<div class="NavHead" style="font-size: 105%; background: transparent; text-align: left; text-align:center;background-color:#efefef;">Lap leaders</div>
<ul class="NavContent" style="list-style: none none; margin-left: 0; text-align: center; font-size: 105%; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; line-height: inherit;"><li style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0"><div class="timeline-wrapper"><map name="timeline_ef187e385314727c9170ddbf7235cf20"></map><img usemap="#timeline_ef187e385314727c9170ddbf7235cf20" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/timeline/ef187e385314727c9170ddbf7235cf20.png" /></div></li></ul>
</div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The <b>2001 Australian Grand Prix</b> (officially the <b>LXVI Qantas Australian Grand Prix</b>) was a <a href="/wiki/Formula_One" title="Formula One">Formula One</a> motor race held on 4 March 2001 at the <a href="/wiki/Melbourne_Grand_Prix_Circuit" class="mw-redirect" title="Melbourne Grand Prix Circuit">Melbourne Grand Prix Circuit</a> in <a href="/wiki/Albert_Park,_Victoria" title="Albert Park, Victoria">Albert Park</a>, <a href="/wiki/Melbourne" title="Melbourne">Melbourne</a>, Victoria, before a crowd of 128,500 people. It was the first round of the <a href="/wiki/2001_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="2001 Formula One World Championship">2001 Formula One World Championship</a> and the 16th edition of the <a href="/wiki/Australian_Grand_Prix" title="Australian Grand Prix">event</a> as part of the Formula One World Championship. The 58-lap race was won by <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Ferrari" title="Scuderia Ferrari">Ferrari</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Michael_Schumacher" title="Michael Schumacher">Michael Schumacher</a> from <a href="/wiki/Pole_position" title="Pole position">pole position</a>. <a href="/wiki/David_Coulthard" title="David Coulthard">David Coulthard</a> of the <a href="/wiki/McLaren" title="McLaren">McLaren</a> team finished second and Schumacher's teammate <a href="/wiki/Rubens_Barrichello" title="Rubens Barrichello">Rubens Barrichello</a> third. It was Schumacher's second Australian Grand Prix win, his fifth consecutive in Formula One and the 45th of his career.
</p><p>Michael Schumacher won the 33rd pole position of his career by recording the fastest lap in qualifying. He maintained the lead until a major accident on lap five involving <a href="/wiki/Williams_Grand_Prix_Engineering" title="Williams Grand Prix Engineering">Williams</a>' <a href="/wiki/Ralf_Schumacher" title="Ralf Schumacher">Ralf Schumacher</a> and <a href="/wiki/British_American_Racing" title="British American Racing">British American Racing</a> (BAR) driver <a href="/wiki/Jacques_Villeneuve" title="Jacques Villeneuve">Jacques Villeneuve</a> resulted in the death of spectator marshal Graham Beveridge, who was struck in the chest by Villeneuve's right-rear wheel. The incident necessitated deploying the <a href="/wiki/Safety_car" title="Safety car">safety car</a>. The race restarted eleven laps later with Michael Schumacher in first place until the <a href="/wiki/Pit_stop" title="Pit stop">pit stop</a> phase for fuel and tyres. Coulthard led for three laps until his stop. Michael Schumacher then regained the lead and maintained it to win the race.
</p><p>Graham Beveridge was the first marshal to die from injuries sustained during a Formula One race since <a href="/wiki/Paolo_Gislimberti" title="Paolo Gislimberti">Paolo Gislimberti</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2000_Italian_Grand_Prix" title="2000 Italian Grand Prix">2000 Italian Grand Prix</a>. His death was investigated by the sport's governing body, the <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A9d%C3%A9ration_Internationale_de_l%27Automobile" title="Fédération Internationale de l&#39;Automobile">Fédération Internationale de l'Automobile</a> (FIA), who concluded it was a "freak accident". A <a href="/wiki/Coroner#Australia" title="Coroner">coroner's report</a> concluded the organisers of the race, the Australian Grand Prix Corporation, were responsible for the accident and it was "avoidable".
</p><p>Following this, Michael Schumacher left Australia as the leader of the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Drivers%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Drivers&#39; Champions">World Drivers' Championship</a> with ten <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Championship_points_scoring_systems" title="List of Formula One World Championship points scoring systems">points</a>. Coulthard was four points behind in second and Barrichello a further two adrift in third. <a href="/wiki/Nick_Heidfeld" title="Nick Heidfeld">Nick Heidfeld</a> of <a href="/wiki/Sauber" class="mw-redirect" title="Sauber">Sauber</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jordan_Grand_Prix" title="Jordan Grand Prix">Jordan</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Heinz-Harald_Frentzen" title="Heinz-Harald Frentzen">Heinz-Harald Frentzen</a> were fourth and fifth. In the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Constructors%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Constructors&#39; Champions">Constructors' Championship</a>, Ferrari led with fourteen points and McLaren were second with eight points. Sauber and Jordan followed in third and fourth with sixteen races left in the season.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Background">Background</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2001_Australian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Background">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:2014_Melbourne_Grand_Prix_(From_Eureka_Skydeck).jpg" class="image"><img alt="An aerial photograph showing the Melbourne Grand Prix Circuit where the race was held" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/2014_Melbourne_Grand_Prix_%28From_Eureka_Skydeck%29.jpg/220px-2014_Melbourne_Grand_Prix_%28From_Eureka_Skydeck%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="131" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/2014_Melbourne_Grand_Prix_%28From_Eureka_Skydeck%29.jpg/330px-2014_Melbourne_Grand_Prix_%28From_Eureka_Skydeck%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/2014_Melbourne_Grand_Prix_%28From_Eureka_Skydeck%29.jpg/440px-2014_Melbourne_Grand_Prix_%28From_Eureka_Skydeck%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3689" data-file-height="2200" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:2014_Melbourne_Grand_Prix_(From_Eureka_Skydeck).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The <a href="/wiki/Melbourne_Grand_Prix_Circuit" class="mw-redirect" title="Melbourne Grand Prix Circuit">Melbourne Grand Prix Circuit</a> <i>(pictured in 2014)</i>, where the race was held.</div></div></div>
<p>The 2001 <a href="/wiki/Australian_Grand_Prix" title="Australian Grand Prix">Australian Grand Prix</a> was the first of the 17 rounds in the <a href="/wiki/2001_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="2001 Formula One World Championship">2001 Formula One World Championship</a> and the 16th Formula One Australian race. It took place on 4 March at the 16-turn 5.303&#160;km (3.295&#160;mi) <a href="/wiki/Melbourne_Grand_Prix_Circuit" class="mw-redirect" title="Melbourne Grand Prix Circuit">Melbourne Grand Prix Circuit</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Melbourne" title="Melbourne">Melbourne</a> suburb of <a href="/wiki/Albert_Park,_Victoria" title="Albert Park, Victoria">Albert Park</a>, Victoria.<sup id="cite_ref-CF12001AusGP_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CF12001AusGP-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> The track is a semi-permanent <a href="/wiki/Road_racing" title="Road racing">road course</a>. Due to the dust laid on it by road traffic all year round, it offers drivers a low amount of <a href="/wiki/Grip_(auto_racing)" title="Grip (auto racing)">grip</a>. Engineers set up the <a href="/wiki/Formula_One_car" title="Formula One car">cars</a> to extract the maximum amount of <a href="/wiki/Downforce" title="Downforce">downforce</a> at the rear and to be stable in high-speed corners. This puts a strain on traction and braking<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> and prompted teams to install cooling devices on the brakes' rotor and <a href="/wiki/Disc_brake" title="Disc brake">calipers</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kimi_Raikkonen_2002_Taiwan.jpg" class="image"><img alt="A photograph of Kimi Räikkönen wearing McLaren overalls in 2002. He was one of four drivers to make their Formula One debut in Melbourne." src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Kimi_Raikkonen_2002_Taiwan.jpg/170px-Kimi_Raikkonen_2002_Taiwan.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="227" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Kimi_Raikkonen_2002_Taiwan.jpg/255px-Kimi_Raikkonen_2002_Taiwan.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Kimi_Raikkonen_2002_Taiwan.jpg/340px-Kimi_Raikkonen_2002_Taiwan.jpg 2x" data-file-width="480" data-file-height="640" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kimi_Raikkonen_2002_Taiwan.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Kimi_R%C3%A4ikk%C3%B6nen" title="Kimi Räikkönen">Kimi Räikkönen</a> <i>(pictured  in <a href="/wiki/McLaren" title="McLaren">McLaren</a> overalls in 2002)</i> was one of four drivers to make their Formula One debut in Melbourne.</div></div></div>
<p>Of the 22 drivers on the starting <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_motorsport_terms#G" title="Glossary of motorsport terms">grid</a>, four made their debut. The <a href="/wiki/1999_CART_season" title="1999 CART season">1999 Championship Auto Racing Teams</a> (CART) champion and <a href="/wiki/2000_Indianapolis_500" title="2000 Indianapolis 500">2000 Indianapolis 500</a> winner <a href="/wiki/Juan_Pablo_Montoya" title="Juan Pablo Montoya">Juan Pablo Montoya</a> joined the <a href="/wiki/Williams_Grand_Prix_Engineering" title="Williams Grand Prix Engineering">Williams</a> team to partner <a href="/wiki/Ralf_Schumacher" title="Ralf Schumacher">Ralf Schumacher</a>, replacing <a href="/wiki/Jenson_Button" title="Jenson Button">Jenson Button</a>, who was loaned to the <a href="/wiki/Benetton_Formula" title="Benetton Formula">Benetton</a> team on a two-year deal.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> At the <a href="/wiki/Arrows_Grand_Prix_International" title="Arrows Grand Prix International">Arrows</a> team, <a href="/wiki/International_Formula_3000" title="International Formula 3000">International Formula 3000</a> (IF3000) participant <a href="/wiki/Enrique_Bernoldi" title="Enrique Bernoldi">Enrique Bernoldi</a> replaced <a href="/wiki/Pedro_de_la_Rosa" title="Pedro de la Rosa">Pedro de la Rosa</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> who lost his race seat and joined the <a href="/wiki/Prost_Grand_Prix" title="Prost Grand Prix">Prost</a> team as test and reserve driver.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> IF3000 driver <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Alonso" title="Fernando Alonso">Fernando Alonso</a> was promoted from a test driver role at <a href="/wiki/Minardi" title="Minardi">Minardi</a> to a race seat.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Kimi_R%C3%A4ikk%C3%B6nen" title="Kimi Räikkönen">Kimi Räikkönen</a>, the <a href="/wiki/2000_Formula_Renault_2.0_UK_Championship" title="2000 Formula Renault 2.0 UK Championship">2000 Formula Renault 2.0 UK champion</a>, drove for the <a href="/wiki/Sauber" class="mw-redirect" title="Sauber">Sauber</a> team in Melbourne, partnering <a href="/wiki/Nick_Heidfeld" title="Nick Heidfeld">Nick Heidfeld</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Many observers, including <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_Racing" title="Jaguar Racing">Jaguar</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Eddie_Irvine" title="Eddie Irvine">Eddie Irvine</a>, Button and the president of the <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A9d%C3%A9ration_Internationale_de_l%27Automobile" title="Fédération Internationale de l&#39;Automobile">Fédération Internationale de l'Automobile</a> (FIA; Formula One's governing body), <a href="/wiki/Max_Mosley" title="Max Mosley">Max Mosley</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-:0_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> criticised Sauber's choice to sign Räikkönen because he had competed in 23 car races prior to his debut and no F1 experience. He took part in a test session at the <a href="/wiki/Circuito_de_Jerez" title="Circuito de Jerez">Circuito de Jerez</a> before 25 FIA commission members for performance analysis in December 2000. Räikkönen was granted a <a href="/wiki/FIA_Super_Licence" title="FIA Super Licence">super licence</a> by a vote of 24 to 1 at a <a href="/wiki/FIA_World_Motor_Sport_Council" title="FIA World Motor Sport Council">FIA World Motor Sport Council</a> meeting on 7 December.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the front of the field, the press considered the 2000 champion <a href="/wiki/Michael_Schumacher" title="Michael Schumacher">Michael Schumacher</a> of <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Ferrari" title="Scuderia Ferrari">Ferrari</a> the favourite to take his fourth <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Drivers%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Drivers&#39; Champions">World Drivers' Championship</a>. <a href="/wiki/Mika_H%C3%A4kkinen" title="Mika Häkkinen">Mika Häkkinen</a> of the <a href="/wiki/McLaren" title="McLaren">McLaren</a> team was predicted to be his nearest challenger.<sup id="cite_ref-SportalPreview_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SportalPreview-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Michael Schumacher arrived with the physiological advantage as Ferrari exceeded its target of completing more than 4,000&#160;km (2,500&#160;mi) in pre-season testing. He said he was confident about his chances in Australia: "The <a href="/wiki/Ferrari_F2001" title="Ferrari F2001">F2001</a> has behaved very well from the first to last day of testing. It has performed brilliantly at <a href="/wiki/Fiorano_Circuit" title="Fiorano Circuit">Fiorano</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mugello_Circuit" title="Mugello Circuit">Mugello</a>. I can say again that never before have I been able to carry out such a preparation in my career and that sends me to Melbourne full of confidence."<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> Häkkinen said the pressure he felt at the start of 2000 increased his desire to win the World Drivers' and <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Constructors%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Constructors&#39; Champions">Constructors' Championships</a> in 2001 and intended to do his best to help McLaren achieve both titles.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The race saw the return of <a href="/wiki/Michelin" title="Michelin">Michelin</a> as a tyre supplier for the first time since the <a href="/wiki/1984_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="1984 Formula One World Championship">1984 season</a>; the company supplied tyres to the Williams, Benetton, Prost, Jaguar and Minardi teams in 2001. They provided Formula One's existing tyre supplier <a href="/wiki/Bridgestone" title="Bridgestone">Bridgestone</a> with competition for the first time since <a href="/wiki/Goodyear_Tire_and_Rubber_Company" title="Goodyear Tire and Rubber Company">Goodyear</a> left following the <a href="/wiki/1998_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="1998 Formula One World Championship">1998 season</a>. The competition led to the development of a tyre where more of its surface area came into contact with the road surface providing the driver with more grip.<sup id="cite_ref-DTTyres_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTTyres-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> This increased the top speeds of cars during pre-season testing and drivers set lap times below 2000-levels to nullify the effect of the reduction in aerodynamic performance and downforce.<sup id="cite_ref-SportalPreview_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SportalPreview-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> It raised concerns within the sport about grooved compounds becoming illegal <a href="/wiki/Racing_slick" title="Racing slick">slick tyres</a>; the FIA declined to enforce a regulation mandating Michelin and Bridgestone to restrict the wear of their tyre compounds.<sup id="cite_ref-DTTyres_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTTyres-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Practice">Practice</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2001_Australian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Practice">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Four practice sessions were held before the Sunday race—two on Friday and two on Saturday. The Friday morning and afternoon sessions each lasted an hour. The third and final practice 45-minute sessions were held on Saturday morning.<sup id="cite_ref-regulations_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> The Friday practice sessions were held in hot and clear weather.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> In the first session, Ferrari's <a href="/wiki/Rubens_Barrichello" title="Rubens Barrichello">Rubens Barrichello</a> was fastest with a lap of 1 minute 29.056 seconds, 0.312 seconds quicker than his teammate Michael Schumacher in second. The two McLarens were third and fourth—Häkkinen ahead of <a href="/wiki/David_Coulthard" title="David Coulthard">David Coulthard</a>. Ralf Schumacher, <a href="/wiki/Jos_Verstappen" title="Jos Verstappen">Jos Verstappen</a> of the Arrows team, <a href="/wiki/Jordan_Grand_Prix" title="Jordan Grand Prix">Jordan</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Heinz-Harald_Frentzen" title="Heinz-Harald Frentzen">Heinz-Harald Frentzen</a>, Montoya, Heidfeld and <a href="/wiki/British_American_Racing" title="British American Racing">British American Racing</a> (BAR) driver <a href="/wiki/Olivier_Panis" title="Olivier Panis">Olivier Panis</a> were in positions five to ten.<sup id="cite_ref-AF1FP1_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AF1FP1-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> While the session was relatively uneventful, Ralf Schumacher and his teammate Montoya ran off the circuit; both drivers avoided sustaining damage to their cars.<sup id="cite_ref-AF1FP1_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AF1FP1-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Barrichello set the day's fastest lap in the second session at 1 minute 28.965 seconds. <a href="/wiki/Jarno_Trulli" title="Jarno Trulli">Jarno Trulli</a> for Jordan, Michael Schumacher, Coulthard, Häkkinen, Ralf Schumacher, Heidfeld, Frentzen, Prost's <a href="/wiki/Jean_Alesi" title="Jean Alesi">Jean Alesi</a> and Panis followed in positions two to ten.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportFP2_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportFP2-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Tarso_Marques" title="Tarso Marques">Tarso Marques</a>' engine failed after seven minutes and laid oil on the track. Both Irvine and Button sustained separate <a href="/wiki/Flat_tire" title="Flat tire">punctures</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-SVFriday_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SVFriday-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Racing_flags#Red_flag" title="Racing flags">Red flags</a> were shown after 35 minutes when Jaguar's <a href="/wiki/Luciano_Burti" title="Luciano Burti">Luciano Burti</a> locked his tyres into the first corner and spun. He damaged the front-left corner of his <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_R2" title="Jaguar R2">Jaguar R2</a> car in an impact with a concrete barrier at the corner's exit. Burti was unhurt.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportFP2_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportFP2-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Frentzen beached his car in the turn six <a href="/wiki/Run-off_area" title="Run-off area">gravel trap</a> with six minutes remaining, and Heidfeld had an off-track excursion, which damaged the front wing.<sup id="cite_ref-SVFriday_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SVFriday-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Shortly after, Michael Schumacher did not see waved <a href="/wiki/Racing_flags#Yellow_flag" title="Racing flags">yellow flags</a> in turn five to alert drivers to Heidfeld. He accelerated and saw the yellow flags in the braking area for turn six.<sup id="cite_ref-SVFriday_23-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SVFriday-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Schumacher lost control of the rear of the car on oil laid on the approach to the right-hand turn six while braking.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> He spun backwards after hitting the inside <a href="/wiki/Curb" title="Curb">kerb</a> and speared into the gravel trap at 120&#160;mph (190&#160;km/h).<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> The wheels dug into a ridge in the gravel on the outside of the turn and the Ferrari lifted airborne. Schumacher somersaulted and barrel rolled twice before landing upright against a tyre barrier. He was unhurt, and he returned to the area later that day to discuss possible changes to turn six after raising concerns the day before.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the third session, Michael Schumacher was fastest in his rebuilt car with a lap of 1 minute 28.134 seconds. The McLarens of Coulthard and Häkkinen were second and third. Trulli was fourth-fastest with <a href="/wiki/Jacques_Villeneuve" title="Jacques Villeneuve">Jacques Villeneuve</a> of BAR fifth and his teammate Panis sixth. Frentzen, Barrichello, Montoya and Irvine followed in the top ten.<sup id="cite_ref-AF1FP3_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AF1FP3-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Barrichello stopped at the side of the track with an engine failure and Verstappen was affected by a <a href="/wiki/Transmission_(mechanics)" title="Transmission (mechanics)">transmission</a> fault caused by an electrical problem.<sup id="cite_ref-FIASaturday_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIASaturday-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Frentzen spun late in the session and avoided damaging his car.<sup id="cite_ref-AF1FP3_27-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AF1FP3-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Coulthard led the final session with a lap of 1 minute 27.540 seconds, followed by Michael Schumacher, Häkkinen, Frentzen, Trulli, Panis, Räikkönen, Irvine and Heidfeld.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportFP4_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportFP4-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> A brake problem caused Marques to spin into the gravel trap and Michael Schumacher stopped at turn six with debris in his left-front brake duct.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportFP4_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportFP4-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Qualifying">Qualifying</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2001_Australian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Qualifying">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Mika_Hakkinen_DTM_Norisring_2009.jpg" class="image"><img alt="A photograph of Mika Häkkinen who was the leading McLaren driver on the starting grid." src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Mika_Hakkinen_DTM_Norisring_2009.jpg/170px-Mika_Hakkinen_DTM_Norisring_2009.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="253" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Mika_Hakkinen_DTM_Norisring_2009.jpg/255px-Mika_Hakkinen_DTM_Norisring_2009.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Mika_Hakkinen_DTM_Norisring_2009.jpg/340px-Mika_Hakkinen_DTM_Norisring_2009.jpg 2x" data-file-width="516" data-file-height="769" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Mika_Hakkinen_DTM_Norisring_2009.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Mika_H%C3%A4kkinen" title="Mika Häkkinen">Mika Häkkinen</a> <i>(pictured as a Mercedes-Benz brand ambassador in 2009)</i> was the leading <a href="/wiki/McLaren" title="McLaren">McLaren</a> driver on the starting <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_motorsport_terms#G" title="Glossary of motorsport terms">grid</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>Saturday's afternoon one hour qualifying session saw each driver limited to twelve laps, with the grid order decided by their fastest laps. During this session, the <a href="/wiki/107%25_rule" title="107% rule">107% rule</a> was in effect, which required each driver to set a time within 107 per cent of the quickest lap to qualify for the race.<sup id="cite_ref-regulations_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> The weather was hot and clear.<sup id="cite_ref-FIASaturday_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIASaturday-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> After a front <a href="/wiki/Camber_angle" title="Camber angle">camber angle</a> alteration,<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Michael Schumacher took his first <a href="/wiki/Pole_position" title="Pole position">pole position</a> in Australia, his fifth in a row extending back to the <a href="/wiki/2000_Italian_Grand_Prix" title="2000 Italian Grand Prix">2000 Italian Grand Prix</a>, and the 33rd of his career with a time of 1 minute 26.892 seconds, almost four seconds faster than Häkkinen's pole lap from the <a href="/wiki/2000_Australian_Grand_Prix" title="2000 Australian Grand Prix">2000 race</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-SundayAgeQuali_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SundayAgeQuali-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DTQuali_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTQuali-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Barrichello in second negotiated slower traffic on his fastest lap; he aborted one lap due to a gear selection fault and was ordered to stop on the <a href="/wiki/Truck_scale" title="Truck scale">weighbridge</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-FIASaturday_28-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIASaturday-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DTQuali_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTQuali-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Häkkinen, who had pole position early on, had balance problems putting him off the track at a bumpy turn one and took third. Frentzen, fourth, was confident in the feel of his <a href="/wiki/Jordan_EJ11" title="Jordan EJ11">Jordan EJ11</a> car, ahead of Ralf Schumacher in fifth, the highest-placed Michelin-shod car.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportQuali_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportQuali-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Coulthard, in sixth, twice ran onto the grass due to car balance problems. Trulli started from seventh, bemoaning a deteriorating handling balance.<sup id="cite_ref-FIASaturday_28-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIASaturday-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DTQuali_33-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTQuali-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Villeneuve took eighth place, ahead of his BAR teammate Panis in ninth; both drivers reported an adequate car balance. Villeneuve collided with Montoya in an attempt to pass him on the inside, necessitating a <a href="/wiki/Bargeboard_(aerodynamics)" title="Bargeboard (aerodynamics)">bargeboard</a> replacement.<sup id="cite_ref-FIASaturday_28-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIASaturday-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Heidfeld in tenth was twice slowed by traffic.<sup id="cite_ref-FIASaturday_28-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIASaturday-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Montoya was the fastest driver not to qualify in the top ten;<sup id="cite_ref-DTQuali_33-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTQuali-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Bernoldi slowed Montoya leaving turn four and put him wide on his final timed lap.<sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Irvine, in his balanced and slightly heavy Jaguar, set the 12th-fastest lap as debris removed one of his bargeboards.<sup id="cite_ref-FIASaturday_28-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIASaturday-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Räikkönen was the highest-placed rookie driver in 13th,<sup id="cite_ref-DTQuali_33-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTQuali-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> as he drove an unbalanced Sauber—a problem his team could not resolve.<sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_35-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Alesi was the faster of the two Prost cars in 14th, as Verstappen's transmission fault prevented him from setting up his car to achieve an optimal performance and was 15th. Button did not have his preferred qualifying setup following a gearbox change and was 16th. His teammate Fisichella was 17th due to a water leak in his car prompting him to switch to the team's <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_motorsport_terms#Spare_car" title="Glossary of motorsport terms">spare car</a>, which had a braking problem.<sup id="cite_ref-FIASaturday_28-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIASaturday-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Bernoldi, 18th, failed to generate sufficient heat into the front tyres on his car with traffic slowing him.<sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_35-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Alonso set the 19th-fastest time in his first Formula One qualifying session; he lost around half a second through an error.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportQuali_34-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportQuali-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_35-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> A strong <a href="/wiki/Understeer_and_oversteer" title="Understeer and oversteer">understeer</a> left Prost's <a href="/wiki/Gast%C3%B3n_Mazzacane" title="Gastón Mazzacane">Gastón Mazzacane</a> in 20th.<sup id="cite_ref-FIASaturday_28-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIASaturday-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Burti in 21st had a left-rear suspension failure sending him into a retaining wall at turn five, stopping the session for 12 minutes to allow track marshals to clear debris.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportQuali_34-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportQuali-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_36-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Occupying the last spot on the grid, Marques failed to set a lap time within the 107 per cent limit due to his unfamiliarity with the <a href="/wiki/Minardi_PS01" title="Minardi PS01">Minardi PS01</a>'s two-pedal setup. He spun at turn three before driving Alonso's race car.<sup id="cite_ref-FIASaturday_28-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIASaturday-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_35-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Minardi appealed to the stewards and Marques was granted permission to start the race under "exceptional circumstances."<sup id="cite_ref-Marques107_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Marques107-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Qualifying_classification">Qualifying classification</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2001_Australian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Qualifying classification">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<dl><dt>Notes</dt></dl>
<ul><li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_1"><b><a href="#ref_1">^1</a></b></span>  – Tarso Marques set a lap time outside the <a href="/wiki/107%25_rule" title="107% rule">107% limit</a>, but he was allowed to start the race.<sup id="cite_ref-Marques107_37-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Marques107-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Warm-up">Warm-up</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2001_Australian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Warm-up">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>A 30-minute warm-up session took place on Sunday morning for teams to set up their cars before the race. It was held in overcast weather with spots of rain that made the track moderately slippery.<sup id="cite_ref-regulations_19-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FIAWarmUp_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAWarmUp-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AutosportWarmUp_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportWarmUp-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> While he was briefly kept in the garage with a suspected engine oil leak,<sup id="cite_ref-FIAWarmUp_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAWarmUp-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Coulthard led the session with a lap of 1 minute 30.099 seconds, 0.053 seconds quicker than his teammate Häkkinen in second.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Verstappen was fastest for the opening 20 minutes before falling to third. Montoya, Panis, Michael Schumacher, Heidfeld, Irvine, Barrichello and Frentzen followed in positions four to ten. After exiting the pit lane at the beginning of the warm-up, Bernoldi lost control of the rear of his Arrows and removed the nose cone from his car in a collision with the turn one wall.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportWarmUp_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportWarmUp-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Race">Race</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2001_Australian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Race">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Coulthard_2007.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Photograph of David Coulthard who finished in second place ffor McLaren." src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/David_Coulthard_2007.jpg/170px-David_Coulthard_2007.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="250" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/David_Coulthard_2007.jpg/255px-David_Coulthard_2007.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/David_Coulthard_2007.jpg/340px-David_Coulthard_2007.jpg 2x" data-file-width="500" data-file-height="734" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Coulthard_2007.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/David_Coulthard" title="David Coulthard">David Coulthard</a> <i>(pictured in 2007)</i> finished in second place for McLaren.</div></div></div>
<p>The race took place before a crowd of 128,500 spectators at 14:00 local time.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GF1RaceReport_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF1RaceReport-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> The weather was dry and overcast with the air temperature between 22 and 23&#160;°C (72 and 73&#160;°F); the track temperature ranged from 27 to 28&#160;°C (81 to 82&#160;°F);<sup id="cite_ref-GF1RaceReport_43-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF1RaceReport-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-F1COMRaceMelbourne_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1COMRaceMelbourne-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> forecasts predicted heavy cloud cover with high humidity and no rainfall.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Tyre durability and grooved tread wear were predicted to affect the race and analysis suggested one pit stop was the ideal strategy for drivers and teams.<sup id="cite_ref-F1COMRaceMelbourne_44-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1COMRaceMelbourne-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Jaguar isolated and fixed a minor vehicle design fault linked to Burti's accident in Saturday's qualifying session. They strengthened the <a href="/wiki/Double_wishbone_suspension" title="Double wishbone suspension">double wishbone suspension</a> on all three of their cars overnight.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Irvine switched to the spare Jaguar due to a <a href="/wiki/Power_steering" title="Power steering">power steering</a> failure on his race <a href="/wiki/Monocoque" title="Monocoque">monocoque</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_36-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Button used the spare Benetton; his mechanics remained on the grid to work on the car before the <a href="/wiki/Parade_lap" title="Parade lap">formation lap</a> began, entailing an investigation by the race stewards resulting in Button incurring a ten-second stop-and-go penalty.<sup id="cite_ref-AtlasF1Race_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AtlasF1Race-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When the five red lights went out to start the race, Michael Schumacher made a brisk getaway to lead going into the first corner.<sup id="cite_ref-SpeedvisionRace_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SpeedvisionRace-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Barrichello in second made a slower start and allowed a pack of cars to approach. Coulthard, on the right-portion, steered to the middle to try and hold off Ralf Schumacher on his left and Frentzen to his right. As the available space was reduced going into the turn one braking area, Frentzen hit the right-hand sidepod of Coulthard's car sending him towards Ralf Schumacher's Williams. He made a second, harder contact that slowed Coulthard.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_36-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Behind the first five drivers, Montoya made up five positions before the end of the start/finish straight.<sup id="cite_ref-AtlasF1Race_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AtlasF1Race-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> He carried too much momentum and drove off the track at turn one.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_36-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Montoya lost several positions and almost made contact with Panis as he rejoined the track.<sup id="cite_ref-AtlasF1Race_2-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AtlasF1Race-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Entering turn three, Montoya attempted to pass Irvine and the two cars collided, sending the Jaguar into the grass and a 180 degree spin.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_36-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GF1RaceReport_43-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF1RaceReport-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> Mazzacane retired with a broken brake pedal and an engine failure.<sup id="cite_ref-AtlasF1Race_2-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AtlasF1Race-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-SpeedvisionRace_47-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SpeedvisionRace-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the conclusion of lap one, Michael Schumacher led Häkkinen by 1.2 seconds and was a further second ahead of Frentzen in third.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_36-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Barrichello challenged Ralf Schumacher for fourth and took the position when the latter ran deep under braking at turn one and fell to seventh. That enabled Coulthard to return to fifth as he had earlier passed Trulli.<sup id="cite_ref-AtlasF1Race_2-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AtlasF1Race-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> On lap two, Bernoldi became the race's second retiree when he lost control of his car exiting turn two and struck the left-hand barrier.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_36-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Barrichello recorded an early <a href="/wiki/Fastest_lap" title="Fastest lap">fastest lap</a> as he moved closer to attempt to pass Frentzen for third.<sup id="cite_ref-F1RacingNet_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1RacingNet-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> On lap three, Barrichello attempted a pass on the right of Frentzen (who was on the <a href="/wiki/Racing_line" title="Racing line">racing line</a> at the time) at turn nine, and the two made contact.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_36-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-F1COMRaceMelbourne_44-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1COMRaceMelbourne-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Frentzen was sent into the grass; he avoided <a href="/wiki/Stall_(engine)" title="Stall (engine)">stalling</a> his engine and rejoined the track in 16th. Barrichello continued in third albeit the <a href="/wiki/Toe_(automotive)" title="Toe (automotive)">toe-in</a> on his front-left wheel was knocked out of alignment.<sup id="cite_ref-F1RacingNet_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1RacingNet-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AF1Quotes_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AF1Quotes-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Further down the order, the lightly-fuelled Verstappen overtook Panis and Heidfeld to move into ninth on the same lap.<sup id="cite_ref-AtlasF1Race_2-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AtlasF1Race-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Marques then joined the list of retirees with a progressively worsening <a href="/wiki/Automotive_battery" title="Automotive battery">battery</a> misfire causing the engine to shut down on lap four.<sup id="cite_ref-AF1Quotes_50-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AF1Quotes-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Jacques_Villeneuve_2002.jpg" class="image"><img alt="A photo of Jacques Villeneuve who was involved in a major accident with Ralf Schumacher that caused the death of a spectator marshal at turn three on lap five." src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Jacques_Villeneuve_2002.jpg/170px-Jacques_Villeneuve_2002.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="255" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Jacques_Villeneuve_2002.jpg/255px-Jacques_Villeneuve_2002.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Jacques_Villeneuve_2002.jpg/340px-Jacques_Villeneuve_2002.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="1500" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Jacques_Villeneuve_2002.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Jacques_Villeneuve" title="Jacques Villeneuve">Jacques Villeneuve</a> <i>(pictured in 2002)</i> was involved in a major accident with <a href="/wiki/Ralf_Schumacher" title="Ralf Schumacher">Ralf Schumacher</a> that caused the death of a spectator marshal at turn three on lap five.</div></div></div>
<p>On lap five, a two-car accident led to the <a href="/wiki/Safety_car" title="Safety car">safety car</a>'s deployment.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> On the approach to turn three at about 290&#160;km/h (180&#160;mph),<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRace_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Ralf Schumacher, on the left, was about to defend from Villeneuve in the centre.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_36-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Villeneuve <a href="/wiki/Drafting_(aerodynamics)" title="Drafting (aerodynamics)">slipstreamed</a> Ralf Schumacher,<sup id="cite_ref-AtlasF1Race_2-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AtlasF1Race-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> and was caught out by him under braking. Villeneuve's right-front tyre struck the Williams' left-rear wheel, launching his car airborne and rotated through 180 degrees towards a retaining catchfence and concrete barrier to his left.<sup id="cite_ref-SpeedvisionRace_47-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SpeedvisionRace-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_48-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> The resulting impact of more than 30<a href="/wiki/G-force" title="G-force">G</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-PitpassNov03_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PitpassNov03-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> and cart-wheeling along the wall, destroyed the rear of Villeneuve's car up to the carbon fibre monocoque. Ralf Schumacher's rear wing was removed and he spun into the gravel trap.<sup id="cite_ref-F1COMRaceMelbourne_44-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1COMRaceMelbourne-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRace_52-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Villeneuve's 38&#160;cm (380&#160;mm) right-rear wheel detached from the car and catapulted through a 40&#160;cm (400&#160;mm) access area.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> It struck the chest of 51-year-old track marshal Graham Beveridge at around 175&#160;km/h (109&#160;mph),<sup id="cite_ref-TCM4Dec01_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TCM4Dec01-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> causing the left <a href="/wiki/Ventricle_(heart)" title="Ventricle (heart)">ventricle</a> of his <a href="/wiki/Myocardial_rupture" title="Myocardial rupture">heart to rupture</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-HSunAPSafer_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HSunAPSafer-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> as well as lung and liver lacerations.<sup id="cite_ref-PMNov03_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PMNov03-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> He was killed instantly.<sup id="cite_ref-TCM4Dec01_55-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TCM4Dec01-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> The force of the impact catapulted Beveridge backwards and clockwise, resting on his back with his eyes open.<sup id="cite_ref-MarshalFlew_58-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MarshalFlew-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> 11 spectators were injured by flying debris.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_36-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>An ambulance was dispatched,<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_36-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> and race officials prevented nearby spectators from forcing their way through a tarpaulin to watch medical personnel tend to Beveridge or scavenge debris.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Beveridge was transported to the track's medical centre and then under resuscitation to the trauma and intensive care unit of <a href="/wiki/The_Alfred_Hospital" title="The Alfred Hospital">The Alfred Hospital</a>, under a protocol established by the local sanctioning body, the <a href="/wiki/Confederation_of_Australian_Motor_Sport" class="mw-redirect" title="Confederation of Australian Motor Sport">Confederation of Australian Motor Sport</a> (CAMS), and the hospital.<sup id="cite_ref-SMHJul03_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SMHJul03-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> He was officially declared dead at 15:08 local time.<sup id="cite_ref-PitpassNov03_53-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PitpassNov03-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> In the meantime, track marshals cleared debris and the remaining drivers conserved fuel at reduced speed behind the safety car. They swerved from side-to-side to maintain warm temperatures in their tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-F1RacingNet_49-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1RacingNet-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_51-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Both Ralf Schumacher and Villeneuve clambered out of their cars unaided.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_51-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Several hours later, Villeneuve admitted himself to hospital, with bruising, muscle damage, nausea and chest pains, mostly due to the pressure put upon him by his car's <a href="/wiki/Seat_belt" title="Seat belt">seat belts</a> in the accident.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Verstappen made a tactical pit stop on lap 15 to support his two-stop strategy. He caught up to the field before the safety car was withdrawn at the end of the lap.<sup id="cite_ref-F1RacingNet_49-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1RacingNet-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Michael Schumacher began to pull away from the rest of the field, increasing his lead by two-tenths of a second per lap.<sup id="cite_ref-SpeedvisionRace_47-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SpeedvisionRace-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> There were overtakes farther down the field. Montoya passed Fisichella for ninth, and Irvine overtook Verstappen and Alonso. Räikkönen passed Button for tenth place on lap 17. Button took his stop-and-go penalty on the next lap.<sup id="cite_ref-AtlasF1Race_2-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AtlasF1Race-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> He emerged at the back of the order.<sup id="cite_ref-F1COMRaceMelbourne_44-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1COMRaceMelbourne-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Michael Schumacher opened up a five-second lead over Häkkinen in second by lap 25.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_36-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Häkkinen retired from the race for the third year in a row on lap 26 with a left-front suspension failure under braking at the end of the back straight sending him backwards into the tyre barrier at Ascari corner.<sup id="cite_ref-SpeedvisionRace_47-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SpeedvisionRace-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_48-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_51-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Häkkinen exited his McLaren with a mild concussion from flying debris striking his helmet and went to the medical centre for a precautionary check-up.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_36-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Michael_Schumacher_01_(sk).jpg" class="image"><img alt="A picture of Michael Schumacher who won his fifth consecutive Grand Prix and the 45th of his career." src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Michael_Schumacher_01_%28sk%29.jpg/220px-Michael_Schumacher_01_%28sk%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="239" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Michael_Schumacher_01_%28sk%29.jpg/330px-Michael_Schumacher_01_%28sk%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Michael_Schumacher_01_%28sk%29.jpg/440px-Michael_Schumacher_01_%28sk%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="991" data-file-height="1077" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Michael_Schumacher_01_(sk).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Michael_Schumacher" title="Michael Schumacher">Michael Schumacher</a> <i>(pictured in 2007)</i> won his fifth consecutive Grand Prix and the 45th of his career.</div></div></div>
<p>With Häkkinen's retirement, Michael Schumacher led his teammate Barrichello by ten seconds and pulled away.<sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_48-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Coulthard started to draw closer to Barrichello albeit momentarily delayed by Fisichella's slower Benetton.<sup id="cite_ref-F1COMRaceMelbourne_44-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1COMRaceMelbourne-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> On lap 31, Panis overtook Trulli for fourth as the latter slowed with a misfiring engine; Trulli soon retired.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_51-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Three laps later, Alonso exited the pit lane following a pit stop and temporarily delayed Barrichello,<sup id="cite_ref-SpeedvisionRace_47-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SpeedvisionRace-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> unbalancing the Ferrari enough to allow Coulthard to stay in his slipstream into turn three. Coulthard steered left and overtook Barrichello into turn four. By this point, Michael Schumacher had extended his lead to 15 seconds and set the race's fastest lap of 1 minute 28.214 seconds on lap 34.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_36-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> He relinquished the lead to Coulthard on lap 37 with his only pit stop for fuel and tyres and rejoined in third.<sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_48-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Barrichello made a pit stop from second two laps later, rejoining the track in fifth.<sup id="cite_ref-AtlasF1Race_2-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AtlasF1Race-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-F1RacingNet_49-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1RacingNet-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A full tank of fuel and traffic meant Michael Schumacher fell 18.1 seconds behind Coulthard until the latter entered the pit lane at the end of lap 41. Coulthard rejoined the race in second, behind Michael Schumacher.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_36-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> After the pit stops, Michael Schumacher led Coulthard by 10.5 seconds. He, in turn, was 10 seconds in front of Barrichello. Panis in fourth pulled away from Heidfeld in fifth.<sup id="cite_ref-GF1RaceReport_43-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF1RaceReport-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> Montoya stopped on the circuit due to an engine failure caused by a broken oil pipe on lap 41, prematurely ending his maiden Grand Prix.<sup id="cite_ref-SpeedvisionRace_47-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SpeedvisionRace-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AF1Quotes_50-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AF1Quotes-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> His retirement promoted Frentzen to sixth.<sup id="cite_ref-AtlasF1Race_2-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AtlasF1Race-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Following a period of stability throughout the field, Verstappen passed Alesi for tenth on the 49th lap.<sup id="cite_ref-AtlasF1Race_2-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AtlasF1Race-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GF1RaceReport_43-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF1RaceReport-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> Four laps later, Button was slowed by a split <a href="/wiki/Exhaust_system" title="Exhaust system">exhaust system</a>. He retired because it overheated his car's electronics.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Michael Schumacher finished first after 58 laps to achieve his fifth consecutive victory and the 45th of his career. Coulthard was 1.717 seconds behind in second with Barrichello a further 31 seconds adrift in third.<sup id="cite_ref-AtlasF1Race_2-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AtlasF1Race-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Panis was fourth on the road, Heidfeld finished fifth and he held off Frentzen in sixth over the last nine laps. Räikkönen, Burti, Verstappen, Alesi, Irvine, Alonso and Fisichella were the final finishers.<sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_48-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-race">Post-race</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2001_Australian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Post-race">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Out of respect for Beveridge's death, the top three drivers on the podium refrained from spraying champagne.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_51-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Michael Schumacher expressed the importance of ensuring he did not push too hard, "Any time I needed to be fast, I was able to go fast, and what is good is that finally we seem to be able to do good starts as well. So all in all, it's the way we wanted to be and for that reason we can obviously be confident for the rest of the season, but obviously we know there is no reason to be overconfident."<sup id="cite_ref-PressConf_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PressConf-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Coulthard said he felt fortunate to finish second after starting from sixth, "I would imagine the team are disappointed, obviously, for whatever the particular problem was with Mika's car, but you've always got to expect some reliability issues in the first race. You hope you can get two cars to the finish, but I don't believe any team would put a lot of money on both their cars making it so far."<sup id="cite_ref-PressConf_63-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PressConf-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Barrichello explained he did not battle Coulthard because of an understeer and was told by Ferrari's technical director, <a href="/wiki/Ross_Brawn" title="Ross Brawn">Ross Brawn</a>, to slow towards the race's end because of fluctuating oil pressure, "It was a difficult race since the beginning, because I had all sorts of troubles."<sup id="cite_ref-PressConf_63-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PressConf-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

.trow{justify-content:center}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .tsingle{float:none!important;max-width:100%!important;box-sizing:border-box;text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .tsingle .thumbcaption{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .trow>.thumbcaption{text-align:center}}</style><div class="thumb tmulti tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:232px;max-width:232px"><div class="trow"><div class="tsingle" style="width:104px;max-width:104px"><div class="thumbimage" style="height:152px;overflow:hidden"><a href="/wiki/File:Olivier_Panis_2002.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Olivier_Panis_2002.jpg/102px-Olivier_Panis_2002.jpg" decoding="async" width="102" height="153" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Olivier_Panis_2002.jpg/153px-Olivier_Panis_2002.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Olivier_Panis_2002.jpg/204px-Olivier_Panis_2002.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2000" data-file-height="3000" /></a></div></div><div class="tsingle" style="width:124px;max-width:124px"><div class="thumbimage" style="height:152px;overflow:hidden"><a href="/wiki/File:Jos_Verstappen_A1_test_2005_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Jos_Verstappen_A1_test_2005_%28cropped%29.jpg/122px-Jos_Verstappen_A1_test_2005_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="122" height="152" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Jos_Verstappen_A1_test_2005_%28cropped%29.jpg/183px-Jos_Verstappen_A1_test_2005_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Jos_Verstappen_A1_test_2005_%28cropped%29.jpg/244px-Jos_Verstappen_A1_test_2005_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1486" data-file-height="1848" /></a></div></div></div><div class="trow" style="display:flex"><div class="thumbcaption"><a href="/wiki/Olivier_Panis" title="Olivier Panis">Olivier Panis</a> <i>(pictured on the left in 2002)</i> and <a href="/wiki/Jos_Verstappen" title="Jos Verstappen">Jos Verstappen</a> <i>(pictured on the right in 2005)</i> had 25 seconds added to their total race times after the stewards deemed them to have passed <a href="/wiki/Sauber" class="mw-redirect" title="Sauber">Sauber</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Nick_Heidfeld" title="Nick Heidfeld">Nick Heidfeld</a> under <a href="/wiki/Racing_flags#Yellow_flag" title="Racing flags">yellow flag</a> conditions.</div></div></div></div>
<p>Sauber team owner <a href="/wiki/Peter_Sauber" title="Peter Sauber">Peter Sauber</a> filed an official appeal with race officials against the BAR and Arrows teams because he believed Panis and Verstappen illegally overtook Heidfeld under yellow flag conditions for Bernoldi's lap two crash. The stewards interviewed the three drivers and reviewed video footage of the incident before upholding Sauber's protest. Panis and Verstappen incurred a 25-second time penalty and dropped from fourth to seventh and ninth to tenth, respectively. This promoted Heidfeld to fourth, Frentzen to fifth and Räikkönen into sixth.<sup id="cite_ref-PanisVilleneuvePenalty_64-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PanisVilleneuvePenalty-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> Panis argued the stewards made an incorrect decision because he felt Heidfeld was overtaken in an area where there were no yellow flags, "What makes me furious is that I was found guilty without any evidence. There was no report from the track marshals and it was all based on accusations made by Nick Heidfeld. It was his word against mine and they said he was right."<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Frentzen felt he missed the chance of taking a podium finish due to the collision with Barrichello albeit unangry about it, saying, "At the end of the day I took away two points for a fifth place spot which, considering how the race went for me, was still pretty good. However, I could have easily been in second place had things gone my way."<sup id="cite_ref-FrentzenBarrichelloCrash_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FrentzenBarrichelloCrash-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> Barrichello argued Frentzen went towards him and affected the toe-in of his left-front wheel.<sup id="cite_ref-FrentzenBarrichelloCrash_66-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FrentzenBarrichelloCrash-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> Frentzen chose not complain about the contact saying, "it wouldn't help anything and I am sure that he is sorry for what he did, especially as it upset the handling of his car for the rest of the race."<sup id="cite_ref-FrentzenBarrichelloCrash_66-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FrentzenBarrichelloCrash-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> Räikkönen was praised by the press and Sauber personnel for his performance.<sup id="cite_ref-GuardianKimi_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GuardianKimi-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TIOSKimi_68-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TIOSKimi-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i><span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">&#39;s</span> <a href="/wiki/Richard_Williams_(journalist)" title="Richard Williams (journalist)">Richard Williams</a> wrote Räikkönen had possibly the best Formula One début of any driver since Villeneuve moved from CART and finished second at the <a href="/wiki/1996_Australian_Grand_Prix" title="1996 Australian Grand Prix">1996 Australian Grand Prix</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GuardianKimi_67-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GuardianKimi-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/David_Tremayne" title="David Tremayne">David Tremayne</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Independent" title="The Independent">The Independent on Sunday</a></i> felt Räikkönen "did not put a wheel wrong all weekend."<sup id="cite_ref-TIOSKimi_68-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TIOSKimi-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Jacky_Eeckelaert" title="Jacky Eeckelaert">Jacky Eeckelaert</a>, Räikkönen's <a href="/wiki/Race_engineer" title="Race engineer">race engineer</a>, said the driver "drove a perfect three days, like a driver who's been doing it for 10 years" and Heidfeld stated he was happy for his teammate.<sup id="cite_ref-GuardianKimi_67-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GuardianKimi-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Five days after the race, Frentzen wrote on his website he was suspicious that Sauber illegally used <a href="/wiki/Traction_control_system" title="Traction control system">traction control</a> (a driver aid outlawed after the <a href="/wiki/1993_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="1993 Formula One World Championship">1993 championship</a>, which was permitted from the fifth round of the 2001 season, the <a href="/wiki/2001_Spanish_Grand_Prix" title="2001 Spanish Grand Prix">Spanish Grand Prix</a>) on their cars to get an unfair advantage.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> He clarified his comments three days later to say the Sauber's fast acceleration out of the tight corners was achieved by an engine software package lowering its power and eliminating <a href="/wiki/Wheelspin" title="Wheelspin">wheelspin</a>, "It cannot be ignored that something like that exists, there is simply no room for discussion about that. On the other hand, however, you can discuss if the device that exists is legal or illegal."<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> Michael Schumacher responded by saying Frentzen had brought Formula One into disrepute and argued the latter should concentrate on his own car and performance, "To make this stupid comment is completely unfair, he should rethink what he is saying. I know he does not say it is illegal but then he has to say that we have done a very good job, not say that it is dubious what we are doing."<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> Frentzen clarified he did not state any car running a Ferrari engine had an illegal traction control system in any media interview or on his website.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As this was the first race of the season, Michael Schumacher led the Drivers' Championship with ten <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Championship_points_scoring_systems" title="List of Formula One World Championship points scoring systems">points</a>. He was followed by Coulthard in second with six points and Barrichello in third with four points. Heidfeld was in fourth with three points and Frentzen was fifth with two points.<sup id="cite_ref-points_73-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-points-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> In the Constructors' Championship, Ferrari collected 14 points because of Michael Schumacher's victory and Barrichello's third-place finish. That gave them an eight-point gap over the second-placed McLaren. Sauber's double points finish placed them third with four points. Frentzen's fifth-place result put Jordan in fourth with sixteen races remaining in the season.<sup id="cite_ref-points_73-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-points-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
